2.1.1.1.3  container vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /vnfm-log:generic-debug/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /vnfm-log:generic-debug/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /vnfm-log:generic-debug/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/vnfm-log:generic-debug/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/vnfm-log:generic-debug/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .vnfm_log.YangNotif.VnfmLog.GenericDebug.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    VnfmLogYang.YangNotif_VnfmLog_GenericDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    VnfmLog__YangNotif__VnfmLog__GenericDebug__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_GenericDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    VnfmLog_notif_GenericDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_GenericDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.3.1.3  container vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /vnfm-log:generic-notice/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /vnfm-log:generic-notice/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /vnfm-log:generic-notice/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/vnfm-log:generic-notice/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/vnfm-log:generic-notice/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .vnfm_log.YangNotif.VnfmLog.GenericNotice.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    VnfmLogYang.YangNotif_VnfmLog_GenericNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    VnfmLog__YangNotif__VnfmLog__GenericNotice__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_GenericNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    VnfmLog_notif_GenericNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_GenericNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.6.1.3  container vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /vnfm-log:vnfm-info/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /vnfm-log:vnfm-info/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /vnfm-log:vnfm-info/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/vnfm-log:vnfm-info/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/vnfm-log:vnfm-info/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .vnfm_log.YangNotif.VnfmLog.VnfmInfo.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    VnfmLogYang.YangNotif_VnfmLog_VnfmInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    VnfmLog__YangNotif__VnfmLog__VnfmInfo__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_VnfmInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    VnfmLog_notif_VnfmInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_VnfmInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.8.1.3  container vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /vnfm-log:internal-error/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /vnfm-log:internal-error/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /vnfm-log:internal-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/vnfm-log:internal-error/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/vnfm-log:internal-error/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .vnfm_log.YangNotif.VnfmLog.InternalError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    VnfmLogYang.YangNotif_VnfmLog_InternalError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    VnfmLog__YangNotif__VnfmLog__InternalError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_InternalError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    VnfmLog_notif_InternalError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_InternalError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.11.1.3  container vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /vnfm-log:vnfm-state-error/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /vnfm-log:vnfm-state-error/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /vnfm-log:vnfm-state-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/vnfm-log:vnfm-state-error/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/vnfm-log:vnfm-state-error/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .vnfm_log.YangNotif.VnfmLog.VnfmStateError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    VnfmLogYang.YangNotif_VnfmLog_VnfmStateError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    VnfmLog__YangNotif__VnfmLog__VnfmStateError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_VnfmStateError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    VnfmLog_notif_VnfmStateError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_VnfmStateError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.13.1.3  container vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /vnfm-log:sonus-vnfm-debug/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /vnfm-log:sonus-vnfm-debug/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /vnfm-log:sonus-vnfm-debug/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/vnfm-log:sonus-vnfm-debug/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/vnfm-log:sonus-vnfm-debug/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .vnfm_log.YangNotif.VnfmLog.SonusVnfmDebug.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    VnfmLogYang.YangNotif_VnfmLog_SonusVnfmDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    VnfmLog__YangNotif__VnfmLog__SonusVnfmDebug__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_SonusVnfmDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    VnfmLog_notif_SonusVnfmDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_SonusVnfmDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.15.1.3  container vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /vnfm-log:cpr-debug/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /vnfm-log:cpr-debug/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /vnfm-log:cpr-debug/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/vnfm-log:cpr-debug/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/vnfm-log:cpr-debug/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .vnfm_log.YangNotif.VnfmLog.CprDebug.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    VnfmLogYang.YangNotif_VnfmLog_CprDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    VnfmLog__YangNotif__VnfmLog__CprDebug__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_CprDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    VnfmLog_notif_CprDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_CprDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.18.1.3  container vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /vnfm-log:cpr-instantiated/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /vnfm-log:cpr-instantiated/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /vnfm-log:cpr-instantiated/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/vnfm-log:cpr-instantiated/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/vnfm-log:cpr-instantiated/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .vnfm_log.YangNotif.VnfmLog.CprInstantiated.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    VnfmLogYang.YangNotif_VnfmLog_CprInstantiated_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    VnfmLog__YangNotif__VnfmLog__CprInstantiated__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_CprInstantiated_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    VnfmLog_notif_CprInstantiated_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_CprInstantiated_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.20.1.3  container vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /vnfm-log:cpr-terminating/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /vnfm-log:cpr-terminating/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /vnfm-log:cpr-terminating/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/vnfm-log:cpr-terminating/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/vnfm-log:cpr-terminating/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .vnfm_log.YangNotif.VnfmLog.CprTerminating.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    VnfmLogYang.YangNotif_VnfmLog_CprTerminating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    VnfmLog__YangNotif__VnfmLog__CprTerminating__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_CprTerminating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    VnfmLog_notif_CprTerminating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.23.1.3  container vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /vnfm-log:vdur-debug/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /vnfm-log:vdur-debug/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /vnfm-log:vdur-debug/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/vnfm-log:vdur-debug/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/vnfm-log:vdur-debug/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .vnfm_log.YangNotif.VnfmLog.VdurDebug.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    VnfmLogYang.YangNotif_VnfmLog_VdurDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    VnfmLog__YangNotif__VnfmLog__VdurDebug__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_VdurDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    VnfmLog_notif_VdurDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_VdurDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.25.1.3  container vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /vnfm-log:vdur-warning/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /vnfm-log:vdur-warning/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /vnfm-log:vdur-warning/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/vnfm-log:vdur-warning/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/vnfm-log:vdur-warning/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .vnfm_log.YangNotif.VnfmLog.VdurWarning.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    VnfmLogYang.YangNotif_VnfmLog_VdurWarning_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    VnfmLog__YangNotif__VnfmLog__VdurWarning__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_VdurWarning_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    VnfmLog_notif_VdurWarning_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_VdurWarning_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.28.1.3  container vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /vnfm-log:security-group-instantiating/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /vnfm-log:security-group-instantiating/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /vnfm-log:security-group-instantiating/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/vnfm-log:security-group-instantiating/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/vnfm-log:security-group-instantiating/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .vnfm_log.YangNotif.VnfmLog.SecurityGroupInstantiating.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    VnfmLogYang.YangNotif_VnfmLog_SecurityGroupInstantiating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    VnfmLog__YangNotif__VnfmLog__SecurityGroupInstantiating__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_SecurityGroupInstantiating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    VnfmLog_notif_SecurityGroupInstantiating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_SecurityGroupInstantiating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.30.1.3  container vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /vnfm-log:security-group-terminating/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /vnfm-log:security-group-terminating/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /vnfm-log:security-group-terminating/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/vnfm-log:security-group-terminating/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/vnfm-log:security-group-terminating/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .vnfm_log.YangNotif.VnfmLog.SecurityGroupTerminating.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    VnfmLogYang.YangNotif_VnfmLog_SecurityGroupTerminating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    VnfmLog__YangNotif__VnfmLog__SecurityGroupTerminating__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_SecurityGroupTerminating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    VnfmLog_notif_SecurityGroupTerminating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_SecurityGroupTerminating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.33.1.3  container vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /vnfm-log:int-vlr-info/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /vnfm-log:int-vlr-info/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /vnfm-log:int-vlr-info/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/vnfm-log:int-vlr-info/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/vnfm-log:int-vlr-info/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .vnfm_log.YangNotif.VnfmLog.IntVlrInfo.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    VnfmLogYang.YangNotif_VnfmLog_IntVlrInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    VnfmLog__YangNotif__VnfmLog__IntVlrInfo__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_IntVlrInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    VnfmLog_notif_IntVlrInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_IntVlrInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.35.1.3  container vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /vnfm-log:vnfr-debug/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /vnfm-log:vnfr-debug/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /vnfm-log:vnfr-debug/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/vnfm-log:vnfr-debug/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/vnfm-log:vnfr-debug/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .vnfm_log.YangNotif.VnfmLog.VnfrDebug.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    VnfmLogYang.YangNotif_VnfmLog_VnfrDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    VnfmLog__YangNotif__VnfmLog__VnfrDebug__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_VnfrDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    VnfmLog_notif_VnfrDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_VnfrDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.37.1.3  container vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /vnfm-log:vnfr-instantiating/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /vnfm-log:vnfr-instantiating/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /vnfm-log:vnfr-instantiating/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/vnfm-log:vnfr-instantiating/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/vnfm-log:vnfr-instantiating/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .vnfm_log.YangNotif.VnfmLog.VnfrInstantiating.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    VnfmLogYang.YangNotif_VnfmLog_VnfrInstantiating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    VnfmLog__YangNotif__VnfmLog__VnfrInstantiating__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_VnfrInstantiating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

  YPBC Base Identifier

2.1.40.1.3  container vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /vnfm-log:vnfr-terminated/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /vnfm-log:vnfr-terminated/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /vnfm-log:vnfr-terminated/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/vnfm-log:vnfr-terminated/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/vnfm-log:vnfr-terminated/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .vnfm_log.YangNotif.VnfmLog.VnfrTerminated.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    VnfmLogYang.YangNotif_VnfmLog_VnfrTerminated_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    VnfmLog__YangNotif__VnfmLog__VnfrTerminated__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_VnfrTerminated_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    VnfmLog_notif_VnfrTerminated_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_VnfrTerminated_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.42.1.3  container vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /vnfm-log:vlr-instantiated/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /vnfm-log:vlr-instantiated/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /vnfm-log:vlr-instantiated/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/vnfm-log:vlr-instantiated/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/vnfm-log:vlr-instantiated/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .vnfm_log.YangNotif.VnfmLog.VlrInstantiated.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    VnfmLogYang.YangNotif_VnfmLog_VlrInstantiated_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    VnfmLog__YangNotif__VnfmLog__VlrInstantiated__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_VlrInstantiated_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    VnfmLog_notif_VlrInstantiated_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_VlrInstantiated_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.45.1.3  container vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /vnfm-log:vdur-instantiating/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /vnfm-log:vdur-instantiating/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /vnfm-log:vdur-instantiating/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/vnfm-log:vdur-instantiating/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/vnfm-log:vdur-instantiating/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .vnfm_log.YangNotif.VnfmLog.VdurInstantiating.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    VnfmLogYang.YangNotif_VnfmLog_VdurInstantiating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    VnfmLog__YangNotif__VnfmLog__VdurInstantiating__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_VdurInstantiating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    VnfmLog_notif_VdurInstantiating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_VdurInstantiating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.47.1.3  container vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /vnfm-log:vdur-terminating/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /vnfm-log:vdur-terminating/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /vnfm-log:vdur-terminating/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/vnfm-log:vdur-terminating/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/vnfm-log:vdur-terminating/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .vnfm_log.YangNotif.VnfmLog.VdurTerminating.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    VnfmLogYang.YangNotif_VnfmLog_VdurTerminating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    VnfmLog__YangNotif__VnfmLog__VdurTerminating__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_VdurTerminating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    VnfmLog_notif_VdurTerminating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_VdurTerminating_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /vnfm-log:volume-info/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /vnfm-log:volume-info/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier

2.1.50.1.3  container vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /vnfm-log:volume-error/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /vnfm-log:volume-error/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /vnfm-log:volume-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/vnfm-log:volume-error/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/vnfm-log:volume-error/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .vnfm_log.YangNotif.VnfmLog.VolumeError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    VnfmLogYang.YangNotif_VnfmLog_VolumeError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    VnfmLog__YangNotif__VnfmLog__VolumeError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers

2.1.52.1.3  container vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /vnfm-log:volume-instantiated/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /vnfm-log:volume-instantiated/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /vnfm-log:volume-instantiated/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/vnfm-log:volume-instantiated/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/vnfm-log:volume-instantiated/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .vnfm_log.YangNotif.VnfmLog.VolumeInstantiated.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    VnfmLogYang.YangNotif_VnfmLog_VolumeInstantiated_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    VnfmLog__YangNotif__VnfmLog__VolumeInstantiated__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_VolumeInstantiated_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    VnfmLog_notif_VolumeInstantiated_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_VolumeInstantiated_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path

  XPath Keyed Path

2.1.55.1.3  container vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /vnfm-log:vnfr-error/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /vnfm-log:vnfr-error/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /vnfm-log:vnfr-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/vnfm-log:vnfr-error/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/vnfm-log:vnfr-error/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .vnfm_log.YangNotif.VnfmLog.VnfrError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    VnfmLogYang.YangNotif_VnfmLog_VnfrError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    VnfmLog__YangNotif__VnfmLog__VnfrError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier

2.1.57.1.3  container vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /vnfm-log:account-debug/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /vnfm-log:account-debug/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /vnfm-log:account-debug/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/vnfm-log:account-debug/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/vnfm-log:account-debug/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .vnfm_log.YangNotif.VnfmLog.AccountDebug.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    VnfmLogYang.YangNotif_VnfmLog_AccountDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    VnfmLog__YangNotif__VnfmLog__AccountDebug__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_AccountDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    VnfmLog_notif_AccountDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_AccountDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.59.1.3  container vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /vnfm-log:datastore-event-debug/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /vnfm-log:datastore-event-debug/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /vnfm-log:datastore-event-debug/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/vnfm-log:datastore-event-debug/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/vnfm-log:datastore-event-debug/vnfm-log:template_params/vnfm-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .vnfm_log.YangNotif.VnfmLog.DatastoreEventDebug.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    VnfmLogYang.YangNotif_VnfmLog_DatastoreEventDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    VnfmLog__YangNotif__VnfmLog__DatastoreEventDebug__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_DatastoreEventDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_VnfmLog_VnfmLog_notif_DatastoreEventDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
